Han, director of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office, previously received a secret report from the people of Rugao County that Wang Zixiang, a company commander of a battalion in a regiment of the office, and Liu Bingxian, a second-in-command, had falsely accused good people of being bandits and extorted large sums of money through illegal means when they were stationed in Rugao last winter. He immediately arrested them and ordered an inquiry. After the victims came forward to provide conclusive evidence, they were executed by firing squad yesterday.

Yangzhou

Liu Chuoan Establishes Soup Kitchen for the Poor 86

Local resident Liu Chuoan and others, recently recognizing that prices are high and that unemployed poor people are struggling to make a living, initiated the establishment of a soup kitchen attached to the Dayuan Shiji Hall in the city. They have also prepared side dishes, charging one copper coin per bowl. The kitchen is scheduled to open in October and has been reported to the Public Security Bureau for the record. They have also requested that police be dispatched to provide protection at that time.

Mingguang

Salt and Grain Merchants Oppose the Collection of Salt and Grain Donations 87

The Fourth District Office of the county previously submitted a request to the county government, which was approved, to collect three cents per package of imported salt and exported grain as an education fund. The collection began yesterday at Sanheji. Salt and grain merchants unanimously opposed the collection, and a conflict occurred, in which the director of the collection, Li Lianbao, was beaten and injured. The office has reported the matter to the county government.

Murder for Money Case Occurs at Yan Jian Bridge 88

At Yan Jian Bridge in Dingzhou, farmer Li Dayou had collected twelve yuan in gifts yesterday for his son's wedding. He hid the money in a bag. As dusk approached and the wedding sedan had not arrived, he went to check. He never returned. A search was launched, and the next morning, Dayou was found lying stiff in a field, with knife wounds and long dead. The money in his bag was gone.

Nantong

Cao Regiment Deploys to Defend Tonghai 89

Cao Pang, commander of the Second Regiment of the Provincial Security Infantry, recently, due to the unrest among bandits in the Tongruhai region, specially dispatched troops to defend the various key land and water passages in the three counties to deter them.

Financial Market in Tongyi in Great Chaos 90

As the new cotton of Nantong came on the market, the financial market suddenly fell into great chaos. Banks and shops uniformly refused to accept banknotes that did not have exchange offices set up in Tongyi, causing those who were unaware of the situation to be shocked and confused. Local businesses, with a certain bank bringing in large amounts of banknotes every day to purchase cotton, the amount of money in circulation in the market has now reached more than six million yuan. Steps are being taken to prevent accidents, and effective relief is being planned.

Jiashan

Discharged Police Officer Causes Trouble on Ship 91

The Zhiyuan, a ship operating between this county and Pinghu, was passing through Dayun Temple Town yesterday (the 30th) when a discharged anti-smuggling police officer boarded the ship. A conflict arose over a minor matter, and the police officer was severely beaten and injured by the ship's crew. When the anti-smuggling squad learned of this, they gathered their colleagues and rushed to the ship to cause trouble. The local Public Security Sub-station sent police to suppress the situation, but it was ineffective. The ship's authorities immediately reported the matter to the Second District of the Waterborne Public Security, requesting assistance. The Second District received the news and dispatched a warship and several patrol boats to the scene to mediate with armed force. The incident was finally brought to an end.

Hangzhou

White Stone Temple Robbery Solved 92

Xu Achuan, a resident of No. 141 White Stone Temple, Pengjiabu, Hangzhou, makes a living weaving silk and has some savings. One day at about 4 PM, six robbers wearing blue short-sleeved shirts and trousers suddenly came, each holding a handgun and a sharp blade, and knocked on the door to enter. Two robbers stood guard at the door, while the other four robbers thoroughly searched the premises. They left after an hour, taking with them two thousand taels of white silk, five bolts of large silk, 122 silver dollars, and a pair of gold earrings, resulting in a loss of more than one thousand yuan. The robbers fled toward Xuanjiabu on Hanghai Road. The Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital received the news and sent telegrams to the various sub-bureaus and outposts to conduct a thorough search. Yesterday (the 2nd) at 6 AM, the case was solved at the home of Zhang Amao at No. 25 Miaodong Village, Qiaosi Township. The original stolen goods, 125 taels of white silk, were recovered. One robber, Liu Jinkui, was arrested, along with two suspects, Zhang Amao and Zhang Lu's family. Liu confessed that he was from Xiaoshan and was a long-term worker at Zhang Amao's home. One day, friends Yang Meisheng, Lu Genyou, and Hao Sheng Lao Cai, Xia Tang Amao and others from Deqing, totaling six people, came to rob. Zhang, the landlord, claimed that he did not know anything. A document has been prepared and sent to the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital for interrogation.

Letter 93

Dear Editor,

I am writing to you regarding the news item in the "Local News" column of your September 24th issue concerning the petition of the County Party members to the Province. Much of it is inconsistent with the facts. After investigation, the transfer of the County Party members has already been regulated by the Provincial Party Department. The County Representative Assembly was held on September 15th. The County Party Department did not receive any clear instructions and therefore had no reason to hold it without authorization. As for the petition of the County Party members to the Province, much of it is also inaccurate. Tingjie personally did not receive any reprimands from anyone. It seems that your local news reporter, in reporting this news, was standing on a particular position, which is detrimental to the value of the news. I am specially requesting that you correct it. Respectfully,

Zhang Tingjie

September 28th

Local News

National Day Celebration During National Crisis 94

The Municipal Government is Ordered to Follow Last Year's Precedent in Commemorative Ceremonies Without Extravagance

After the Central Standing Committee decided on the method for celebrating the Double Tenth Festival this year, the Executive Yuan issued an order to the entire country not to be extravagant and to follow last year's precedent. The Municipal Government received a telegram from the Executive Yuan yesterday stating that the Central Standing Committee has decided on the method for celebrating the Double Tenth Festival this year. Celebrations in the country should follow last year's precedent, while celebrations abroad should be held as usual. A day off will be given on that day. During this period of national crisis, the commemorative ceremonies held in the country should not be extravagant. In terms of publicity, the National Day Commemoration Publicity Outline and Publicity Points issued by the Central Propaganda Committee should be followed consistently. The Executive Yuan, with the seal of Wang Zhaoming, has issued an order for strict compliance. The Municipal Government, after receiving the telegram, has issued an order to all its affiliated agencies to comply.

League of Nations Technical Liaison Officer Dr. Rajchman Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 95

Representatives from the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Finance Welcomed Him

Met with Finance Minister Song Ziwen in the Afternoon for Detailed Talks

Scheduled to Travel to the Capital Today with Finance Minister Song

Dr. Rajchman, a special commissioner for technical cooperation dispatched by the League of Nations, arrived in Shanghai on the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso yesterday with his secretary. He immediately met with Finance Minister Song Ziwen and is scheduled to travel to the capital with him tonight. Details are listed below:

Arrival Situation 96

The Italian ship Conte Rosso, carrying Dr. Rajchman and others, entered port at around 11 AM yesterday and docked at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong at 12 noon. Li Dijun, Director of the Information Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yu Ming, Director of the Foreign Affairs Office, Dr. Malay, Representative of the League of Nations, and Welsh, an attaché of the Polish Legation, were among those who welcomed him at the wharf. Tang Hai'an, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the National Economic Council, Li Ting'an, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, and Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai University, also traveled to the ship on a small launch from the Harbor Quarantine Station to welcome him. After Dr. Rajchman was inspected by a doctor from the Harbor Inspection Office, he and Tang Hai'an, Qin Fen, and others boarded the small launch from the Harbor Quarantine Station and crossed the river.

Dr. Rajchman arriving in Shanghai yesterday (photographed by Gong Shuxian)

He disembarked at the Bund Wharf on Beijing Road at 12:45 PM. As a result, the representatives from various parties who went to the Qichang Wharf to welcome him, as well as Chinese and Japanese journalists, did not get to meet with Dr. Rajchman. In addition, Guo Dehua, Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, went to the Jianghai Customs Wharf to welcome him but also failed to meet him.

Accompanying Personnel 97

Only Secretary Dr. Marks and Mr. Glonfell accompanied Dr. Rajchman on the ship to Shanghai yesterday. In addition, Dr. Pasik, the League of Nations representative in Shanghai, had traveled to Hong Kong to welcome him and arrived with Dr. Rajchman. Furthermore, Professor Tandel, a friend of Dr. Rajchman, is also arriving in Shanghai to take up a professorship at a university.

Meeting with Minister Song 98

After disembarking at the Bund on Beijing Road, Dr. Rajchman, accompanied by his secretary, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tang Hai'an, and Secretary-General of the National Economic Council Qin Fen, traveled by car to Song's residence on Qiqi Road at 1:10 PM to meet with Finance Minister Song Ziwen. Qin left after sending Dr. Rajchman and others to Song's residence, while only Tang stayed at Song's residence to accompany them and had lunch there. Song and Rajchman talked until about 4 PM before dispersing. Dr. Rajchman and his secretary then went to the Cathay Hotel on the Bund to rest.

Dr. Rajchman's Remarks 99

A reporter visited Dr. Rajchman at the Cathay Hotel yesterday for a very brief conversation. Dr. Rajchman, due to the large number of visitors and his reluctance to deal with them, stated that he was a civil servant and could not say much when meeting with Chinese and foreign journalists. However, he has largely decided to enter the capital in a very short period of time to pay respects to the key figures of the National Government and to contact the National Economic Committee regarding everything. He met with Finance Minister Song Ziwen this afternoon (yesterday afternoon). He declined to answer any other questions from reporters. It is said that Finance Minister Song will travel to the capital with Dr. Rajchman tonight.

Mission to China 100

Dr. Rajchman, a Polish national, is the Minister of Health of the League of Nations. He was invited to China several years ago to guide health construction. He returned to Europe last year to report. This summer, after Finance Minister Song arrived in Geneva, the League of Nations decided to send him to China as a technical cooperation liaison officer. His mission is to: (1) report to China on the actual situation of the League of Nations' various technical institutions and how they can assist China in construction; (2) transmit to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations the Chinese government's needs for various technical cooperation to send additional technical personnel to China to assist in its implementation; (3) when the Chinese government needs technical cooperation for construction projects, the liaison officer should provide as much assistance as possible, attend meetings of the National Economic Committee, and report on the League of Nations' various technical actions; (4) the liaison officer should submit a detailed report to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations at least once every three months on the progress of his technical cooperation assistance in China.

Relief Workers of Various Charity Groups Report on Disaster Relief Efforts in Henan Province by Telegraph to Shanghai 104

Hua County's Fifth, Sixth, and Seventh Districts Hit Hardest

Request Approval from Ministry of Communications for Free Telegrams in Disaster Areas

The joint association of various Shanghai charities for raising emergency relief funds for the Yellow River flood disaster received a telegram yesterday from Mingdao and Zhang Zepu, relief workers in Henan Province, reporting on the disaster relief efforts and requesting that the Ministry of Communications be requested to approve free telegrams in the disaster areas. The original text is as follows: "Dear members, I have sent two telegrams after arriving in Bian, which should have reached you. Master Hongsan is staying in the province waiting for funds and contacting various matters. Zepu and Dao, together with the relief workers, rushed to Hua County on the 25th. The territory of the county is divided into ten districts. The fifth, sixth, and seventh districts were the hardest hit. They are now departing in groups, visiting the disaster areas in person, and bringing the prepared disaster-affected household registers to conduct on-site investigations and distribute aid separately so that the people can receive real benefits and the funds are not wasted, so as not to fail the trust of the benefactors. The six relief workers, Ma Shushan, Wei Lengwei, Chen Hairu, Zhang Chen, Zhang Qixian, and Hu Hanwen, along with the two monks Zhiguang and Zhengbo from the Henan Buddhist Association, and layperson Wang Yixuan, rushed to the disaster area in Hua County. This letter is prepared and submitted for your review. Also, the issued free telegram license states that it is to be sent from Kaifeng. If it is in other counties, it will be restricted. If a telegram is required for important matters, it is necessary to travel thousands of miles to and from the provincial capital, which is both costly and arduous, and it is very inconvenient. It is requested that this association request the Ministry of Communications to approve its universal use in the disaster areas to facilitate progress. This is the prayer. Mingdao and Zhang Zepu, respectfully."

Mayor Wu Officially Assumes Additional Position as Garrison Commander Yesterday 105

Simple Ceremony, Encouraging Staff to Serve Peacefully

Zhang Xiang resigned, Jiang Qun Succeeds as Chief of Staff

Mayor Wu Tiecheng went to the Longhua Garrison Command at 10 AM yesterday to officially assume his concurrent position as acting commander. Inauguration Situation 106

Mayor Wu assumed the additional position of acting commander. Photo of Commander Wu taking office (photographed by Xu Tianzhang)

Wu's Address 108

Wu, the acting commander, then gave a speech: "Chief of Staff, honored guests, colleagues, I have been ordered by the government to be the acting commander of the Songhu Garrison Command. I did not notify the association or my friends beforehand and only came here to take office during the memorial week ceremony. I am the mayor and the acting commander. In taking office, on behalf of the citizens, I express my gratitude for Commander Dai's past achievements. Shanghai is a major port in the East, and its importance is second to none in the country. During the January 28th Incident and in the two years since, the ability to maintain security during wartime and restore order after the war, allowing the lives of the citizens of this city to quickly return to normal, is all due to the fact that Commander Dai, Chief of Staff Zhang, and all the staff have been responsible and hardworking. These achievements should be remembered by everyone. As mayor, I represented the citizens and expressed my appreciation when Commander Dai left. Now that I have been ordered by the government to be the acting commander, I am deeply ashamed and fearful of my lack of talent and ability. After taking office, I can only follow the precedents and adopt Commander Dai's past good practices and do my best to consolidate Shanghai's security and maintain Shanghai's order."

Zhang and Wu's Instructions 109

Finally, acting Chief of Staff Zhang Xiang first gave instructions to all the staff, saying, "After Mayor Wu became the acting commander, he strongly urged me to stay, and I am very grateful. However, due to various reasons, I plan to take a temporary rest. Today, I am taking leave of you all. In addition to working hard, I hope you will not forget my two words: 'Work hard in your position' and 'Specialize in your duties.' These are the words that I have always told you. They are my farewell message to you." Then, Mayor Wu gave instructions, saying, "After I take office, I hope you will all work peacefully and support me with the same spirit that you supported Commander Dai."

Appoint New Staff 110

After Wu took office, he went to the commander's office to take up his duties and began to work. He then announced the list of new staff: Chief of Staff Jiang Qun, Adjutant Wen Jiangang, Chief of Staff Luo Weixiong, Chief of Military Law Tao Baichuan, Chief of Administration Song Dazhang, etc., have all been officially announced. Zhu Haishan, Deputy Captain Rui Qingrong, and Peng Bowei have also been internally appointed as Captains of the Detective Team. However, Chief of Staff Luo Weixiong is still in Guangdong Province, and a letter has been sent to notify him. Before he arrives, Wen Jiangang will temporarily act as his agent. Wu Daonan will be the Director of the Office.

Report from Wang Gongjue's Letter to the Support Association Regarding the War Situation, Requesting Assistance 113

Wang Gongjue, Commander of the Third Route Army of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, recently instructed the communication office stationed in Shanghai from the front lines to present a letter to the Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, reporting on the war situation and requesting assistance. The letter reads: "With utmost respect, since the September 18th Incident, our various units have been engaged in anti-Japanese operations. After years of bloody battles, we have suffered significant sacrifices. Currently, the First and Second Columns of our command, numbering approximately 18,000 men, are still stationed in the Rehe-Western area, participating in the recovery of lost territories. However, we are severely lacking in both pay and ammunition, and our supplies are often insufficient. Although the officers and soldiers have endured great hardships, they are still able to persevere and fight bravely. The recent details of our engagements are briefly outlined as follows: On the 25th of this month, five enemy aircraft suddenly appeared to reconnoiter our position at Mojiazi in Rehe-Western area. On the following day at dawn, Binmu Saburo led an artillery regiment to cover the advance of the puppet troops under Chen Tianzhu. Our troops ordered the entire First Column to engage the enemy resolutely, and then dispatched a 500-man broadsword team, along with heavy machine guns, to charge the enemy. Taking advantage of the momentum, we launched a full-scale assault, and the enemy gradually collapsed and retreated. Due to our lack of food and ammunition, we dared not pursue them. In this battle, we captured one Japanese officer named Inoue and three puppet officers. The enemy suffered over 300 casualties, while our own losses were even heavier. The seriously wounded officers and soldiers have been sent to the rear for medical treatment by Adjutant Lai Debiao and others. However, the enemy continues to attack from time to time, not only causing devastation to nearby villages, which is unbearable to witness, but also resulting in numerous casualties among our troops, which is truly painful to speak of. What troubles us most is that the weather is gradually turning cold, and many of our soldiers still lack cotton clothing. Combined with the shortage of food and ammunition, we are in a state of extreme anxiety. We earnestly implore you all to find a way to provide relief, so that the officers and soldiers at the front can muster their remaining courage to fulfill their patriotic aspirations with their blood. If you grant us your guidance, please send it to the communication office stationed at No. 410, North Lane, Cihou, Hartung Road, Shanghai, for forwarding, as our various units are currently engaged in battle at the front and have no fixed address." With utmost respect, this is specially presented to the gentlemen of the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, including Elder Zi, Elder Jing, Elder Shao, and Elder Hui. Wang Gongjue, Commander of the Third Route Army of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, and Yang Xianfu, Chief of General Staff, along with all officers and soldiers, respectfully submit this on September 26th.

Two Installments of Arrears Paid Continuously in Two Batches 114

Amounting to a Total of More Than 997,000 Yuan

The Jinghu Railway was in arrears to the China and British Corporation for interest on bonds for more than eighteen years, with a total amount of 498,839.2 yuan. Initially, only 100,000 yuan had been paid. It was not until this year's settlement of arrears that 270,000 yuan was first paid on August 11th. Recently, on September 26th, another 128,839.2 yuan was paid, thus clearing the entire debt. Furthermore, the Huhangyong Railway was in arrears to the China and British Corporation for the principal of the 18th term loan, totaling £37,500, which was due on May 18th, 1932. Initially, no payment was made. On August 9th of this year, £25,000, equivalent to 400,000 yuan, was first paid. Recently, on September 29th, another £12,500, equivalent to 198,196.72 yuan, was paid, thus clearing the entire debt as well.

Expansion of the Electricity Workers' Strike 121

Workers at Both the New and Old Factories Began a General Work Stoppage Yesterday Morning

Dagongshe reports that the labor dispute involving the work stoppage of workers at the new factory of the Shanghai Electric Power Company has not been resolved due to the company's persistent attitude. Over 800 workers at the old factory also began a work stoppage yesterday morning in response, and the labor unrest is becoming increasingly serious. Details are recorded as follows:

Old Factory Responds to Work Stoppage After the workers at the Yangshupu New Factory of the Electric Power Company declared a work stoppage on the 29th, they were refused entry to the factory the next morning, and the company's attitude remained strong. To show their support, the workers at the old factory, after deliberation by the work stoppage committee, decided that all 800+ workers would also respond and join the work stoppage yesterday morning. It was learned in advance that the factory would similarly refuse entry, so to avoid conflicts with the factory and other unfortunate incidents, they will not enter the factory for the time being. In total, there are over 2,000 workers at the two factories. Except for the power generation section, which continues to operate as usual, the work in all other departments has completely stopped.

Promulgation of Work Stoppage Discipline The work stoppage committee, in order to regulate the workers' actions, issued the following work stoppage discipline yesterday: (1) During the work stoppage, the work stoppage committee is the highest authority; (2) All workers at the new and old factories should absolutely obey the orders and directions of the work stoppage committee; (3) During the work stoppage, all workers should strictly maintain order and not act outside the rules; (4) During the work stoppage, it is forbidden to fabricate rumors and disrupt people's minds; (5) During the work stoppage, all workers should patiently wait for the resolution of the dispute and not deliberately panic or shrink back; (6) During the work stoppage, all workers should not go to the factory to watch; (7) During the work stoppage, each worker should go to the designated location to inquire about news and not believe rumors; (8) Workers who do not comply with the above discipline will be considered traitors; (9) Those who are willing to be running dogs or traitors will be severely punished.

Preparedness of the Two Factories Since the workers at the new and old factories announced a general work stoppage, the factory, in order to prevent workers from causing trouble, had the Dongting Road gate of the Yangshupu New Factory in Pudong guarded by multiple Chinese and Indian police officers. Other factory gates entering and exiting Yangshupu Road were also guarded by two Chinese police officers each, with strict security measures. However, since the workers implemented the work stoppage, they did not enter the factory yesterday because the factory refused them entry. The workers at the old factory also went to the Municipal General Labor Union yesterday morning to hold a meeting, and the order was excellent.

White Russians Begin Work After the workers at the old factory on Feilun Road joined the work stoppage yesterday morning, the company, fearing that the dispute would be prolonged and disrupt power generation, immediately hired over 50 White Russians to enter the factory in preparation for replacement. In the Yangshupu New Factory, Russian workers were assigned to various parts, such as the furnace room, internal and external coppersmith rooms, cold working room, blacksmith room, coal hoisting room, and wire picking room, to start work yesterday. According to Zhuang Zhishun, a worker in the power generation room, who spoke to a Dagongshe reporter, although the factory hired Russian workers to replace them, in fact, the White Russians lacked experience and needed two people to replace one Chinese worker. Currently, the power generation section has not yet received orders from the work stoppage committee, so it is still working as usual to maintain the current. If the factory does not realize this, the over 200 power generation workers will definitely go on strike automatically to achieve final victory. At that time, even if the factory hires White Russians to replace them, it will be difficult to avoid problems in maintaining power generation.

Petitioning the Party and Government for Assistance The labor unions of the water and electricity industries in the four districts dispatched representatives Ni Tianfu, Dong Shengquan, Chen Youfa, and others yesterday morning to petition the municipal government. Because Mayor Wu was inaugurated as the garrison commander yesterday, all the responsible persons of the departments went to participate, and no one received them. They then went to the municipal party headquarters to petition, and Dai Youheng of the People's Movement Department received them and promised to consult with the standing committee and then coordinate with the Social Affairs Bureau to mediate. Finally, they went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau General Labor Union to make the same petition, requesting assistance. Their petition is as follows: A petition is hereby submitted by representatives, requesting your review and approval, and that you grant us assistance to uphold justice and promote fairness. The members of our union, the workers of the Shanghai Electric Power Company, have been subjected to oppression under the oppression of imperialism. Since June of last year, the company has repeatedly dismissed large numbers of workers and refused to pay the meritorious service funds transferred from the former Public Works Department. Their oppression of the workers has reached its extreme. This time, when the Hua directors were mediating on the dismissal of four workers, Ni Wenfu, Pan Genlin, Zhang Caisheng, Chen Baogen, and others, the company authorities took advantage of the situation and dismissed three workers, Dai Renheng, Xue A'bao, and Yin Binggen, on the pretext of laziness without evidence. Their intention to undermine the labor movement is very obvious. All the workers could no longer bear it and had no choice but to endure the pain of a work stoppage. However, considering that electricity is a public utility and relates to social order, which is extremely important, we still maintain power generation, implying the intention of maintaining social order while urging the capitalists to realize their error. However, the company authorities, relying on their imperialist power, are behaving arrogantly. The future outcome is difficult to predict, and a more serious dispute may arise as a result. The company shall bear the responsibility for this. Therefore, we are specially writing this document and sending Yang Zhaogeng and others to state the facts. We humbly request your office to quickly adopt effective measures and grant us a review and decision, which would be greatly appreciated. Respectfully submitted to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Headquarters, and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau.

Zhong Si's Mediation is Ineffective The electricity workers petitioned Zhong Si, the Director-General of the Public Works Department, last Saturday. Zhong received them and promised to consult with the Electric Power Company, instructing them to go there yesterday to await a reply. The workers still sent representatives Zhu Haosheng, Zhang Changsheng, Bao Defu, Zhu A'fu, and others yesterday morning to meet with Huidekui. Huidekui instructed them to go in the afternoon. The representatives went again at 4:30 PM to await a reply. Huidekui, representing Zhong Si, formally replied to the workers, stating that Zhong had consulted with the company authorities, but the company's attitude was quite insistent and there was still no concrete solution. He hoped that all the workers would resume work immediately to avoid expanding the dispute. The representatives returned to the union to report to the workers.

The Labor Union Writes to the Public Works Department The labor union of the water and electricity industries in the four districts wrote to the Public Works Department yesterday, saying, "With utmost respect, our union members used to serve in the electrical department of your bureau. There was sincere cooperation between us, and your bureau was also able to sympathize with the workers' pain and treat them equally. The workers were able to have a stable life and worked diligently, so there were no accidents. After the Shanghai Electric Power Company took over the electrical department, it turned this public utility into a private profit-making organization, and frequently oppressed our hard-working workers. In the three years since the takeover, it has dismissed more than 500 workers and destroyed the benefits that your bureau had established for the workers. In April of this year, it dismissed four workers, Ni Wenfu, and others, without reason. Although our union repeatedly requested the enthusiastic mediation of Hua directors Yu Qiaqing, Xu Xinliu, Yuan Ludeng, and Wang Xiaolai, the chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the company authorities dismissed workers Xue A'bao and Dai Renheng, who had served for many years, on the pretext of laziness, and also dismissed Qiu Binggen because he was sick and took more than three days of leave. They also refused to pay the 5% meritorious service fund stipulated by the former electrical department of your bureau, claiming that the company had the right to arbitrarily change the regulations. We believe that using the words 'laziness without evidence' and 'overdue sick leave' as excuses for dismissal is not only without legal basis but also contrary to human sentiment. We fear that no other country in the world has such regulations. Moreover, it is even more unreasonable to refuse to pay the meritorious service fund that the workers have accumulated over the years with their sweat and blood. All the members of our union believe that the company's actions are unreasonable and illegal. Therefore, we have had no choice but to endure the pain of a work stoppage. However, considering the importance of the electricity business to society, we still maintain power generation, and our internal organization is strict, and our actions are orderly. We will never act inappropriately. Our union and your bureau have an old relationship as loyal supporters, and we dare to ask you to take a fair stand and grant us assistance. We are anxiously awaiting your response."

The Company Issues a Statement The Shanghai Electric Power Company issued an English statement, which is excerpted and translated as follows: "At 8:00 AM on the 29th of last month, the workers at the Yangshupu New Factory of our company suddenly went on strike. The factory had not received any prior notice. Our factory has always treated workers with tolerance. This sudden strike, which affects social safety, was unexpected. Before that, the workers had not made any representations to the managers of our factory. Even on the evening of the 29th of this month, the factory was still isolated from news and had not received any letters from the workers stating the reasons for the strike. Our company believes that electricity is a public utility and has a great responsibility to society. Therefore, we have repeatedly advised workers not to strike without reason, which would endanger the local area, and for the safety of all workers, we declare that labor and management should not strike arbitrarily until there is no solution to any negotiations. This time, the workers suddenly went on strike, neither declaring it clearly nor discussing solutions with the factory. The responsibility for this to the local area and the public must be borne by

The Citywide Union Declares The Shanghai Postal Union and over ninety other labor unions issued a declaration of support yesterday for the electricity workers' work stoppage, saying, "International capitalists, relying on their abundant capital and the unequal treaties as their protection, are not only expanding their economic power in our country but also repeatedly oppressing our hard-working workers. Past facts have been recognized by people across the country. The workers of the American Shanghai Electric Power Company work hard and contribute their blood and sweat to international capitalists, working like cattle and horses. What they earn is only enough to keep them warm and fed, and they spend the whole year hoping to get 5% of their pension. Now, the company authorities have disregarded their conscience and dismissed workers one after another on the pretext of slow business, and they also intend to swallow up the pension that the former Public Works Department had agreed to pay. The workers of the factory, under this iron heel, have repeatedly groaned and cried out, but have failed to move the company authorities to pity them. Moreover, they despise our party and government organs and refuse the mediation of our Hua directors, resulting in a tangled dispute that has not been resolved. They regard our Chinese workers as cattle and horses and treat our Chinese people as nothing. This is truly outrageous. This time, the workers of the new and old factories have implemented a work stoppage to fight strongly against international capitalists for the sake of national status and the dignity of the workers. This struggle is not comparable to ordinary labor-management disputes, nor can it be compared to other labor unrest. Our union, from a national standpoint and out of solidarity with the same class, vows to do its utmost to provide support. We hope that people from all walks of life will rise up and provide strong assistance. Then the nation will be fortunate, and the workers will be fortunate. This is our declaration. The Shanghai Postal Union, the labor union of the water and electricity industries in District 1, the labor union of the cigarette industry in District 4, the labor union of the water and electricity industries in District 6, the labor union of the shipbuilding industry in District 1, the lumber industry labor union of steamships, the waiter labor union of the Huhang steamships, the labor union of the soap and medicine industries in District 9, the labor union of the cotton textile industry in District 7, the postal workers' union, the labor union of the public bus industry in District 6, the labor union of the cotton spinning industry in District 10, the labor union of the shipbuilding industry in District 5, the hard slice industry union, the military uniform union, the southern goods industry union, the sauce industry union, the toothbrush union, the wine-making industry union, the labor union of the cotton spinning industry in District 5, the labor union of the rubber industry in District 4, the medicine industry union, the pharmaceutical industry union, the leather-making union, the labor union of the cosmetics industry in District 1, the labor union of private boat carpenters, the automobile drivers' union, the inland steamship union, the labor union of the British-American factories, the labor union of the cleaning industry in District 4, the labor union of the paper-making industry in District 5, the dyeing industry union, the fresh pork union, the candle industry union, the rice measuring union, the lithographic printing union, the labor union of the cotton textile industry in District 6, the labor union of the paint-making industry in District 6, the electrical union in District 4, the labor union of the cotton spinning industry in District 3, the labor union of the cleaning industry in District 7, and over ninety other labor unions jointly declare."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Writes to the Public Works Department, Asking it Not to Approve the Telephone Company's Price Increase 122

Protect the Public Interest Based on the Contract

How Can They Request a Price Increase If the Design is Poor?

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce wrote to the Public Works Department yesterday, asking it not to approve the telephone company's price increase. The original letter is recorded below: "With utmost respect, recently, Shanghai newspapers published news that the Shanghai Telephone Company will again increase its prices. As soon as the Public Works Department of the Public Concession approves it, it will announce the measures. This is deeply shocking. According to the contract signed between the company and your bureau, the company may increase prices after the automatic switchboard is completed and the number of Ansen's report is increased. It may not increase prices again within three years. That is to say, even if the company is currently suffering losses, it should be restricted by the contract and may not request a price increase arbitrarily. Your bureau also has the responsibility to protect the public interest based on the contract and may not approve it arbitrarily. Moreover, the reason for the company's business losses, according to a careful investigation by the public, is actually due to its poor design. For example, the number of lines actually in use is only more than 40,000, while there are 100,000 lines of equipment. This means that the estimate is too broad. For an enterprise of more than 20 million taels, only one-quarter of the capital is raised, and the rest is raised by issuing bonds and borrowing to carry out activities, resulting in increased debt interest. All these inappropriate handling situations cannot require the public to increase their burden to compensate for them. Your bureau seeks the interests of the citizens in the concession, not the interests of a private company. The citizens, in view of the approval of the telephone company's price increase last year, believe that this matter has become a serious problem. How your bureau will handle this matter has caused a lot of anxiety among the citizens and has to give its advice in advance. To the Public Works Department of the Public Concession."

Methods to Convert Companies' Capital from Taels to Yuan 123

Should be Submitted by the Competent Authority for Filing

Since the implementation of the abolition of taels and the conversion to yuan, all companies whose capital was previously denominated in taels have converted to national currency. However, when applying for registration of the change after implementation, many difficulties often arise. It is heard that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in order to avoid these difficulties, has formulated three alternative methods and ordered the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to follow them. After receiving the order, the Social Affairs Bureau, in addition to following them, also ordered the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to notify them to follow. The details of the methods are as follows: (1) The total amount of company shares converted from taels to yuan, calculated at a fixed rate of 715, with 10,000 taels converted to 14,000 yuan, should be submitted by the competent authority for filing, without the need to apply for registration of the change; (2) The amount of each share converted at a fixed rate of 715, with 10 taels converted to 14 yuan, should be submitted by the competent authority for filing, without the need to apply for registration of the change; (3) Reissuing shares, or adding a stamp to the shares to indicate the change, is up to the company's discretion.

The newly elected committee members and the incumbent committee members will then elect five standing committee members, and one chairman will be elected from the five. Now the election materials are ready and displayed on the spot. The number of member representatives present has reached the legal quorum, and the drawing of lots can begin. Please invite the representatives from the Party Department, Social Affairs Bureau, and Chamber of Commerce to deliver speeches to emphasize the importance of the election." Then, Zhu Yakui from the Municipal Party Department, Hu Yuqi from the Social Affairs Bureau, and Wang Yansong from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce successively delivered speeches. Representatives' Standing Committee Meeting: At the first 24th members' representatives standing committee meeting, Chairman Qin Runqing reported on (1) the minutes of the previous meeting, (2) incoming and outgoing documents for September, with 43 incoming documents and 972 outgoing documents, (3) 16 joint meetings of the same industry were held at this association in September, (4) according to a letter from member Qian Yuan Fu Ji Zhuang, due to the impact of the current situation, it announced liquidation, (5) various reports on the reserve.

Matters for Discussion: (1) The interbank lending rate for September was requested for public resolution, which was decided to be two yuan. (2) According to a letter from member Yong Xing Zhuang, changing shareholders, the original shareholder Chen Zifang withdrew one share, and from October 1st of this year, Yu Zhendong added half a share, and Chen Huozhou added half a share, which was submitted to the temporary executive committee yesterday for review and approved, and submitted to the general meeting for decision according to regulations, which was resolved and passed. (3) Approval of the proposal by the 48th executive committee of the first session to amend the articles of association of the Money Trade Joint Reserve, please ratify the amendment to Article 18 of Chapter 5 of the Shanghai Money Trade Joint Reserve Articles of Association, "This reserve shall have one manager, who shall be appointed by the executive committee. The manager shall consult with the chairman and standing committee members to handle all daily tasks." After the Merger of the Two Exchanges, All Gold Brokers Oppose It 126

After the Shanghai Goods Exchange merged its securities section with the China Merchants Securities Exchange, the gold section had repeatedly consulted with the Gold Exchange. Due to the relationship between the rights of both parties and the difficulty in controlling the brokers, the merger had not been resolved. Recently, Mr. Du Yuesheng and Mr. Zhang Xiaolin took on the role of mediators and proposed that the names of the original two exchanges be canceled and a new exchange be jointly established to be the only financial market in Shanghai. The capital amount was set at 2 million, which would be contributed equally by both parties, with the principle of equal reciprocity. This was agreed upon by Yu Qiaqing, the chairman of the Goods Exchange, and Xu Pusheng, the chairman of the Gold Exchange. The contract was signed on the 24th of last month to resolve the case. However, all 139 gold exchange brokers believed that the gold exchange chairman Xu Pusheng had not consulted them beforehand, believing that this move not only violated the principle of merger but also damaged the interests of all brokers. A general meeting was immediately convened, and a unanimous resolution was passed to oppose it. In addition to sending nine representatives to negotiate with Chairman Xu and explain everything to the mediators, they also telegraphed the Ministry of Industry to appeal for remedy. The details are as follows:

Telegram to the Ministry of Industry 127

The Gold Exchange Brokers Association of Shanghai telegraphed the Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing: "Chen, the Minister of Industry, it is our pleasure to obey the order to merge the two exchanges, the Gold Exchange and the Goods Exchange, within a specified period, as it concerns government orders. However, Chairman Xu of our exchange did not consult all brokers beforehand and directly negotiated specific conditions with the Goods Exchange to contribute equally and reorganize, and also jointly telegraphed your ministry with the Goods Exchange. This matter not only violates the merger order, but the result is that it greatly damages the interests of all of us. According to legal facts, it does not comply. A meeting has been held to deny it unanimously. We publicly elected representatives to urgently negotiate with Chairman Xu and dare to quickly declare to your ministry to ensure that our original rights and interests are not subject to unexpected losses. We are deeply grateful. In addition to submitting a detailed statement separately, we will telegraph in advance and await your instructions. The Shanghai Gold Exchange Brokers Association, all 138 people, including Wang Jiafu, Tian Derun, Zhan Liansheng, Ge Zhifen, Zhang Zhusun, Wang Yingchang, You Shuren, etc., respectfully bow."

Negotiation Situation 128

Yesterday morning, nine representatives of the Gold Exchange Brokers Association, including Ge Zhifen, Tian Derun, and Zhang Zhusun, went to the Gold Exchange on Jiujiang Road Bund to meet with Chairman Xu Pusheng to handle the negotiations. Chairman Xu received them. First, the representatives stated their intentions, briefly saying that Chairman Xu had signed a contract with the Goods Exchange without consulting all the brokers regarding the merger of the Gold Exchange and the Goods Exchange, and the conditions negotiated greatly damaged the interests of the brokers. The brokers found it difficult to approve this merger method and requested that the original interests of the brokers be effectively taken care of to comply with the law. Then, Chairman Xu replied, expressing complete acceptance of the representatives' opinions and saying that the original interests of the brokers would be effectively taken care of. If the brokers had any opinions on the existing merger method, he would do his best to ensure that it did not violate the order and did not harm the original interests of the brokers. The representatives were satisfied and returned. In the afternoon, the representatives went to Du Yuesheng and Zhang Xiaolin, the two mediators, to explain everything and request sympathy and assistance. It is heard that Du and Zhang have agreed to convene the relevant parties again for further discussion.

Important Notice 129

The Gold Exchange Brokers Association issued an important notice saying, "We have learned that the two exchanges, the Gold Exchange and the Goods Exchange, have repeatedly received orders from the government to merge within a specified period, which is a government order, and we are happy to comply. However, Chairman Xu of our exchange did not consult all of us beforehand and disregarded our original rights and interests, and directly negotiated specific conditions with the representatives of the Goods Exchange on September 24 to reorganize with the method of equal contribution, and directly telegraphed the Ministry of Industry with the Goods Exchange. This move not only violates the principle of merger, but the result is that it greatly damages the interests of all of us. (Omission in the middle) Therefore, we issue an important notice that until a proper and fair method is negotiated by this association, this association does not recognize any actions taken by Chairman Xu that harm the rights and interests of all members of this association. We hereby solemnly declare."

The Shantou Wharf Labor Dispute Resolved 131

The Drug Store Dock Resumes Shipping on the 5th

The drug industry dock workers in this city declared a strike on the 10th of last month in protest against the Shantou merchants, Hong Taixing, and others, for undermining the wharf labor standards. The strike has lasted for nearly a month. The Drug Material Industry Association, because the strike of the dock workers has affected the operations of various firms, specially convened both parties for mediation the day before yesterday. It was immediately decided that the Shantou merchants should still handle matters in accordance with the wharf labor regulations set by the dock workers, and a resolution was announced. All dock workers are approved to resume shipping on the 5th of this month. The Lawyers Association Advises Members Not to Attack Each Other 132

If Unavoidable, First Request Mediation from the Association

The Shanghai Lawyers Association yesterday issued a notice to all members, saying, "Dear members, according to a letter from member Zhang Henghai, the number of members in our association has been increasing in recent years, the rule of law has been promoted, and talents have emerged, which is gratifying. However, members have forgotten their agency status, benefited from others, and attacked each other, even publishing it in newspapers, causing social criticism, and scandals have emerged endlessly, which is regrettable and hateful. Lawyers may also notify the parties to terminate their entrustment for legal acts they want to promise. Article 16 of the Lawyers' Regulations has already clearly stipulated this. If the opposing lawyer is also an agent, then they are both qualified as agents. They should be happy to shake hands and exchange greetings, and do their best for their clients. They can engage in legal disputes, right and wrong, but why involve irrelevant matters outside the case, add fabrications to the agent, attack arbitrarily, or hide behind the scenes, instruct the parties to do so, or act as an accomplice, joining the vortex, disregarding the parties' true goals, and not hesitating to use innuendo to attack colleagues who protect human rights. According to legal human feelings and lawyer ethics, this is absolutely inappropriate. Even our provisional rules clearly prohibit this. Our members believe that the bad trend has started and is even worse now. If we do not quickly seek to eliminate it and let it happen again and again, the impact will not only make the attackers happy and lose their personality, but also the overall members and the future of the rule of law will inevitably suffer adverse consequences. With a member's heart feeling dangerous, they have to inform. They specially propose to send a letter to all members advising them not to attack each other. If it is absolutely necessary, they should first send a letter to the Executive Supervisory Committee of this association to hold a fair mediation. If the mediation fails and the dispute continues, they should try to prevent the wrong party from proceeding with their illegal acts and send a letter to the Executive Supervisory Committee members to promptly discuss whether it is appropriate to implement it. It has been submitted to the Executive Supervisory Committee for discussion and resolution. All members should be notified to check and file the case. Correspond accordingly and hope that your members will check and act accordingly."

Guanling Township, Xiqu District, Yin County, Reports a Disaster 133

Chen Hongyuan, the head of Guanling Township in the 7th District of Yin County, sent a letter to the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association, saying, "To the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, with respect, our township is located in the Yinjiangqiao area of Yin County, surrounded by mountains on all sides, with barren land and poor people. Since the mountain flood in the 10th year of the Republic of China destroyed roads, we were grateful to the elders of your association for donating generously to provide disaster relief and restore the old appearance. The villagers have been praising it to this day. Unexpectedly, at 4:00 p.m. on September 17th of this year, a hurricane and torrential rain replayed the strange disaster. The pond embankments, roads, and bridges were all washed away, and the flood flooded, almost turning into a swamp. The most severely affected was Xueyan'ao, because the village pond embankments and roads along the stream were all washed away. The cost of urgent repair is estimated to be more than 5,000 yuan. Secondly, the left and right lines of Dongnan Liangken. The left line road was less damaged, but all the bridges collapsed. The right line was low-lying, and there were not many bridges and roads along the stream. The estimated repair cost is about 3,000 yuan. Again, the roads along the stream in Shanshang and Jia'ao were also collapsed a lot, with an estimated repair cost of more than 800 yuan. If the main road is along the Ginkgo tree under Wu Jia'ao and other places, they are fortunate to escape the disaster, but the collapse of walls is no less than other villages. However, because of the continuous autumn rain after the disaster, the rice seedlings have sprouted, which has become a disaster. Therefore, we sincerely ask the elders of your association to generously donate and provide assistance to the victims. We will be extremely grateful."

Large-Scale Drug Manufacturing Organization Cracked on Huining Road in Nanshi 136

A Wholesale Distribution Center Was Seized on Mayuan Street

A Large Amount of Drugs and Machines Were Confiscated

| Seven Principal Offenders, Including Zhan Kanglin, Were Arrested |

Zhan Kanglin, a native of Huizhou (26 years old), had no steady employment. Recently, he colluded with accomplices Zhan Qingting (42 years old), Zhu Qiankun (55 years old), Wu Yuezhong (35 years old), Hong Zibing (41 years old), Wu Hansheng (35 years old), Cheng Neng (27 years old), and other fellow villagers to secretly establish a manufacturing

Red Pill Drug 137

factory at No. 9 Shundeli, Huining Road, Nanshi, and set up a wholesale distribution center for red pills at No. 32 Mayao Lane, Mayuan Street, near the City God Temple in the city. It specialized in retail and wholesale to various places in this city and other cities. The business was very developed and profitable. In addition to daily expenses, Zhan and others divided all the income among themselves. Because the matter was not kept secret and the spoils were not distributed evenly, it was discovered by Li Xiaobao and Fang Lingen, the investigation leaders of the Second District of the Public Security Bureau. They reported the information to Captain Lu and Li, the head of the Second District in charge. The team dispatched Zhang Kun, Jin Yushan, Yang Bingsheng, Shi Chunlin, Wang Yingliang, Gu Rusheng, Cheng Peizhang, and other large numbers of investigators and patrol officer Zhou Zhicheng, fully armed, to secretly surround No. 9 Shundeli, Huining Road, at midnight yesterday. Zhang Kun and Jin Yushan, two investigators, climbed over a wall more than ten feet high to open the door and swarm in. Zhan Qingting and Zhu Qiankun were fast asleep and were arrested on the spot. After interrogation, Zhan confessed that this place was a red pill manufacturing factory, and the wholesale distribution center was located at No. 32 Mayao Lane, Mayuan Street, in the city. Various red pill manufacturing equipment was seized, including a red pill rolling machine, a copper mold board, a copper sieve, three bamboo sieves of various sizes, a powder grinding jar, a magnetic basin, a tin box, a large scale, a stick,

a box of raw material powder, and many other miscellaneous items. The witnesses were taken to the district office for detention. The investigators then escorted Zhan to the red pill wholesale distribution center at No. 32 Mayao Lane, and met with Liu Yunfang, the head of the second office of the first district in charge. The police were dispatched to arrest Zhan Kanglin, the red pill boss, and Wu Yuezhong, Wu Hansheng, Cheng Neng, and four others. More than 20,000 red pills, three bags of raw material white powder, and large and small bags of egg powder, three large and small boxes for storing red pills, and more than 80 paper bags, and large and small balances were also seized. They were immediately taken to the district office, and District Head Li interrogated the suspects. All the suspects directly admitted to manufacturing and selling red pill drugs. Zhan and others also confessed that the shareholder Hong Zibing was also the principal, responsible for

purchasing raw materials and controlling the secret recipe, and was currently hiding at No. 31 Baokang Lane, Avenue Joffre. After verifying the confession, District Head Li instructed Li Xiaobao and others to cooperate with Chinese and Western detectives from the Songshan Road Police Station of the French Concession to secretly arrest Hong Zibing (41 years old), a Huizhou shareholder of red pills, in the reception room of No. 31 Baokang Lane at about 3:00 a.m. yesterday. After filing the case at the Xibutou in Lujiawan, they brought him back at 10:00 a.m. At 2:00 p.m., the Second District prepared a document and sent the seven suspects and evidence to the General Bureau for legal investigation.

Hagenbeck Circus's Land and Sea Animals Arrive 138

There are over one hundred species in total.

Never before seen in Shanghai.

Arriving at the port this afternoon.

The German Hagenbeck Circus is world-renowned. Besides wild animals, the troupe also has a large number of marine animals, all of which can perform. This time, they came from Germany to the Far East to perform, first to Japan, then to China, and then to India. The troupe has over one hundred land and sea beasts. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai today. The situation is reported as follows:

Coming to Shanghai after Performing in Japan: The German Hagenbeck Circus is very famous in Europe and America. This time, coming to the Far East to perform, they first arrived in Yokohama, Japan, and then in Kobe and other ports, performing for about two months. On September 2nd, due to a strong wind, the troupe's tent was blown down, causing a major panic about wild animals escaping. The Hagenbeck troupe has now finished performing in the Orient and has taken a steamer from Japan to Shanghai. They will perform in Shanghai for forty-two days before going to India to perform.

Jardine Matheson Handles Everything: The troupe's trip to the Far East for performances was pre-arranged with Jardine Matheson, who agreed to manage everything in China and Japan. Therefore, when departing from Germany, all the troupe's performers, wild animals, etc., traveled directly to Yokohama on Jardine Matheson's "Saarland" steamer. Now, coming to Shanghai, Jardine Matheson's giant steamer "Duisburg" transported all the troupe's animals and personnel from Japan to Shanghai and also handled animal import, performance affairs, and various advertising matters in Shanghai. Preparations have been completed in recent days. The theater is located on the open space opposite the Dahua Hotel.

The Beasts Arrive in Shanghai Today: The wild animals in the Hagenbeck troupe, including tigers, lions, zebras, leopards, deer, polar bears, black bears, etc., are divided into thirty-two large carts, with each cart further divided into several cages. In addition, there are thirty-one large horses, fifteen small horses, five giant elephants, six camels, and another four guanacos. There are also twenty intelligent dogs. Furthermore, there are many marine animals, such as seals and sea tigers, as well as a type of seabird. The ostriches and various beasts are transported using nine motorized vehicles and twenty-six non-motorized vehicles, as well as thirty-two large boxes. All the performers, props, etc., are transported from Japan by Jardine Matheson's "Duisburg" steamer and are expected to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon, disembarking at the Kung Wo Hong Wharf.

Scheduled Performance Dates: The troupe plans to rest for three days after arriving in Shanghai, using this time to set up the theater. The official premiere is scheduled for the 7th of this month, with performances scheduled for six weeks, a total of forty-two days. After the Shanghai performances, Jardine Matheson will transport the troupe to Mumbai, India, for performances before returning home. Although the arrival of the troupe's animals in Shanghai today is for performances, the Jianghai Customs, for strict preventive measures, has ordered the troupe to first pay a deposit of 20,000 yuan. This fee will be returned when they leave Shanghai after the performances. If there are any sales of animals, import duties will be levied according to regulations.

Murder Case Arises from a Brawl Over Fishing Nets 139

Wang Shengren Beats Wei Shengsheng to Death

Wang Shengren, a fisherman from Zhenjiang, was laying nets to catch fish at the Nanjing Road wharf on the Huangpu River on the night of the 9th of last month. Coincidentally, his colleagues, Wei Shengsheng, Wei Rongsheng, Wei’s sister Cai Wei, and clan member Wei Maojian, all from Pudong, were also casting nets in the river at the same location. Wang, wanting to get ahead, moved the nets to a different location, hoping to catch more fish. Wei Shengsheng felt that Wang’s irregular competitive tactics were unacceptable and confronted him. This started with a verbal argument and escalated into a physical fight. Wei Shengsheng was punched in the lower back. Rongsheng and others intervened to break up the fight. At the time, Shengsheng did not feel any pain. However, the next morning, his injuries suddenly worsened. He rushed to his sister Cai Wei's house at 614 Miller Road in the American Settlement to tell her what happened. She sent him to the Renji Hospital, where doctors immediately administered treatment, but it was impossible to save him. He died from his injuries. The police station took the body to the forensic examination office on Fieland Road for an official autopsy. They ordered the body to be prepared for burial and also launched an investigation to apprehend the murderer and bring him to justice. Last Saturday, Geng Debiao, a detective from the General Police Station, and detective Ni Jiaxin learned that Wang Shengren was hiding in the Nanshi area. They went to the fish market on Jiangyin Street to apprehend Wang. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Local Court. Presiding Judge Qian Hongye conducted the preliminary hearing. Attorney Qian Xunjiu from the police station presented the case. Wei Rongsheng and others were present to testify. When questioned, the defendant only admitted to the argument and denied punching Wei Shengsheng. The court stated that the case still needed to be investigated and ordered the defendant to be detained pending further questioning.

The Navy's Three Transport Ships Converted to Merchant Vessels 143

Jing'an Purchased by Sanbei

Pu'an and Ke'an Leased to China Merchants

The Navy Department plans to sell three transport ships. Pu'an has already been leased to China Merchants. Jing'an has now been purchased by Sanbei, and Ke'an is also under negotiation with Liu Hongsheng. The situation is reported as follows:

Jing'an Sold: Among the Navy's three transport ships, Jing'an is the most suitable for commercial use. Although Pu'an has many passenger seats, it does not have cargo holds, making it unsuitable for commercial routes. This ship has already signed a lease contract with China Merchants to continue the Qingdao route and is currently under repair. In addition to passenger seats, Jing'an can also carry over one thousand tons of cargo. Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan initially contacted China Merchants and also planned to lease it to the bureau for routes in northern China. Zhou Houkun, the deputy director of the shipping department, went to Beijing to inspect the ship. However, due to the lease price, an agreement was not reached. Yu Qiaqing of Sanbei Company, aiming to develop coastal routes, contacted Minister Chen to purchase the Jing'an. After discussion, the price was reportedly agreed at 260,000 yuan. The two parties have agreed, and payment and delivery of the ship will take place soon. Jing'an has 2,400 tons, with first, second, and third-class passenger seats and cargo holds, and good speed.

Ke'an to be Leased: Ke'an transport ship is similar to Jing'an, but with a shallower draft, making it most suitable for navigating the Zhejiang coastal routes. After Haiyan was ordered to cease operations, China Merchants found that Jiahe was not suitable for the Wenzhou route. Therefore, the repaired Guangji is currently operating on that route. At the same time, China Merchants has been contacting the Navy Department to discuss leasing the Ke'an. Negotiations have been going on for several weeks. Now, Liu Hongsheng has directly discussed the terms of leasing Ke'an with Minister Chen. It is reported that the two sides are close to reaching an agreement. Once the lease contract is signed, the bureau will take over the ship, make some repairs, and then operate the Wenzhou route. According to Minister Chen's intention, the Ke'an should be sold to China Merchants. It is said that the bureau is sympathetic to this idea and will start with a trial lease.

Russian Émigré Groups in Shanghai Send Representatives to the Mainland to Raise Funds 144

To aid Elderly Émigrés

A letter to this newspaper from the Shanghai Russian Émigré "Elderly Émigré Relief Society" reads: "Dear Sir, Our fundraising representative, Mr. Astakhov, recently returned to Shanghai after raising funds in Guangdong, Macau, Shantou, and Xiamen. According to his returned donation register, it is evident that the people of your country are charitable and generous in their donations. The representative also stated that the donors from all walks of life are deeply concerned about the elderly members of our society. We are extremely grateful for the support we have received. However, the members of our society are all in their seventies and eighties, unable to work, and will need much more assistance in the future. Therefore, our society is now sending Mr. Astakhov, with his donation register, receipt book, permit, registration certificate, articles of association, etc., to raise funds in other parts of your country. We hope that all kind-hearted people will show compassion, regardless of boundaries, and contribute money or clothing so that the elderly members of our society do not become homeless. Sincerely, Popov, President of the Elderly Émigré Relief Society, 967 Avenue Joffre."

Merchants Selling Bottled Colored Wine Granted Exemption from Re-Taxation 145

Approved by the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance

The Shanghai Liangshao Wine Industry Association previously stated that the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance stipulated that merchants selling bottled colored wine also had to pay additional taxes, resulting in double taxation and hindering business. The Association sent representatives He Xiangsheng, Ni Yangzhou, Lu Xingjie, and Zhu Shirong to the Department to submit a written petition, explaining the difficult situation and requesting exemption from re-taxation to alleviate merchants' difficulties. The Taxation Department has now approved: "Two petitions regarding the request for exemption from re-taxation on bottled colored wine and the deputation of representatives to present the difficult situation have been received. This case was previously reported by the Jiangsu Stamp and Wine Tax Bureau, requesting the revision of two items of the tax standards for locally produced fruit and herbal wines. The first item concerns the collection of taxes from local wine manufacturers and home brewers, who will be taxed at the rate of 3.2 yuan per hundred jin, the same as that of sorghum wine. The second item concerns merchants who purchase locally produced wine on which fixed-rate taxes have already been paid and then modify it into various colored wines, who will be exempt from paying additional taxes. This has been approved by the Ministry and will be implemented accordingly. It is also stipulated that all stores that sell locally produced wine and also modify it into colored wine must report the estimated quantity and names of the colored wines they will produce throughout the year to the local tax collection agency within a specified period for verification and registration. All such stores will not be issued separate certificates for the containers of colored wines that have been modified from originally taxed wines. If they need to be transported to other places in the province or to other provinces for sale, the merchants should prepare an application, send it to the local tax collection agency for verification, and issue a transportation permit. These measures will be implemented starting from October 1 of this year. The Jiangsu Bureau is ordered to comply. You are hereby ordered to inform all merchants in the same industry. The forms for the application have also been prescribed by the Ministry and sent to the Jiangsu Bureau for printing and distribution to each sub-bureau for use. When selling the aforementioned modified colored wine, the merchants should obtain an application form from the local tax collection agency, fill it out clearly, and submit it for verification and issuance of a transportation permit, which will be used for verification along the way, as the colored wine imported from other provinces should still be taxed at the fixed rate of 3.2 yuan per hundred city jin in accordance with the regulations. This approval, etc." It is also heard that the Association, after receiving the approval, has notified all its members to comply.

Newly Discovered Ancient Sutra Title 147

Never Before Recorded

The Song Edition Sutra Printing Society at 714 Weihaiwei Road has strived for perfection in its printing of Song Qisha Sutras. They have sought and compared various printing plates from far and near, and have discovered one or two dozen versions. Recently, Dharma Master Fan Cheng obtained hand-scroll copies of Sutras from Guangsheng Temple in Shanxi to supplement the Qisha Sutras. Ye Gongchuo recently invited Zhu Qinglan, Xu Naichang, Jiang Weiqiao, Dong Kang, Zhang Yuanji, Xia Jingguan, Zhao Zunyue, Yuan Tongli, and others to his residence to exhibit and study these ancient Sutras. Dong Kang determined that they were engraved in the early Northern Song Dynasty. Zhang Yuanji said that the characters were slightly angular, suggesting that they were engraved in the Southern Song or Jin Dynasty, but the engraving method and printing paper were all from the Northern school, which was generally recognized by the others. There are currently over five thousand volumes of these Sutras, which have never been recorded in public or private collections, making them extremely valuable. It has been decided to reprint them, defining a single typeface. The printing will be done by the printing society in Beijing and Shanghai, and the parties are already in contact. Someone mentioned that they had read Sutra scrolls with 22 lines of 18 characters per page, 23 lines of 14 characters, 25 lines of 26 characters, and 31 lines of 21 characters. The ends of the paper had a long red stamp that read "Monk Zu Mei, Head of the Sutra Printing Society." Although there is no date or temple name, the people who provided the funds for engraving can be identified. Thirteen excerpts are listed below for public viewing. Note: The Great Tang Records on the Western Regions, Hezhong Prefecture, Yishi, Linghu Village at the foot of the slope. Xiangbei Dispute Mediated in Shanghai Yesterday 148

Negotiations to Continue Today

The Shanghai National Medicine Industry Association had a dispute with the Ningbo Yaojiang Xiangbei Cooperative over the transport and sale of Fritillaria cirrhosa, as has been previously reported. Zhang Shenzhi and Fang Jiaobo, prominent figures from Ningbo in Shanghai, mediated the dispute. Yesterday (the 2nd), they convened representatives from the three parties at the Yong'an Company's Great Eastern and Western Restaurant to resolve the issue. Those present included Zheng Jiahao, Xu Youheng, and Cui Gongzhang, directors of the Yaojiang Xiangbei Cooperative, Cai Tonghao, Chen Chuxiang, and Tong Guangfu, members of the Shanghai Pharmaceutical Industry Association, and Weng Yangqing, a representative of the Ningbo Pharmacy. Also present were Mu Xizhang, a member of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction stationed at the Yaojiang Xiangbei Cooperative, and Ye Mei, a cooperation instructor from Yinxian. At the meeting, Chairman Zhang Shenzhi and Fang Jiaobo gave speeches encouraging peaceful resolution and preventing escalation. Subsequently, Xu Youheng, a representative of the Yaojiang Xiangbei Cooperative, and Cai Tonghao, a representative of the National Medicine Industry Association, both made earnest statements expressing their willingness to reconcile. Mu Xizhang, the Zhejiang Construction Department representative stationed at the cooperative, provided a thorough explanation of the regulations for Fritillaria cirrhosa prices and the Shanghai pharmaceutical industry's misunderstandings of the Fritillaria cirrhosa cooperative. Next, Weng Yangqing, the representative of the Ningbo Pharmacy, expressed his willingness to terminate the sales contract with the cooperative to avoid external misunderstandings. The cooperative stated that termination of the contract required a replacement; otherwise, the current sales relationship would create practical difficulties. Finally, it was decided that representatives from the three parties would go to the Ningbo Shanghai Native Place Association at 2:00 PM today (the 3rd) for further negotiations, with the goal of eliminating prejudices and achieving a satisfactory resolution. The meeting adjourned in harmony after 2:00 PM.

Huashouli House Demolition Dispute Landlord Actually Cuts Off Water Supply 149

Tenants Claim Lease Not Expired

Issue a Declaration Seeking Assistance

The Shanghai Municipal Council felt that the Huishan Small Vegetable Market was too small to accommodate the public and wanted to build a larger vegetable market to benefit vegetable vendors and residents. After surveying, they found that the location of Huashouli opposite the vegetable market was most suitable. They consulted with the owner, the British firm Sickber & Co., and proposed to exchange the land, with the Municipal Council paying Sickber & Co. 32,000 taels of silver. Sickber & Co. felt that this move by the Municipal Council was also for the benefit of the citizens and did not refuse. They accepted the exchange terms. The Municipal Council notified all tenants of Huashouli on August 29th, giving them one month to move out to facilitate the handover. After receiving the notice, the tenants of the neighborhood claimed that when the houses were completed in 1922, all tenants had spent three months' rent and digging fees, ranging from 1,000 to 2,000 yuan per household, or at least 600 to 700 yuan. The landlord verbally agreed to a 20-year lease. Counting the years, only eleven years have passed. Now, they are using the excuse of renovating the small vegetable market to force them to move, which is an unreasonable oppression. They asked the legal advisor of the Huashouli Tenants' Association, lawyer Jiang Chiping, to formally inquire with the Municipal Council whether the vegetable market renovation was actually happening. Until the deadline for relocation arrived the day before yesterday, there was still no reply. Just as they were hesitating, Sickber & Co., seeing that the tenants were still residing there and not preparing to move, knew that it could not be resolved by peaceful means and decided to cut off the water supply first to force them to comply. Therefore, all the tenants became more and more panicked. In addition to negotiating with the water company to continue supplying drinking water, which the company understood and agreed to, they also issued a declaration seeking social assistance. However, the Municipal Council's plan to build a wide vegetable market on the site has been finalized, and it is feared that the tenants will eventually have to move.

A Notorious Bandit Committed a Kidnapping Case in Zhenjiang 150

The Police Are Chasing Accomplices and Investigating the Location of the Hostage

Wang Chengying and Yang Xiguang, Chinese detectives from the Jiading Road Police Station, arrested notorious bandit Pan Xiuliang, Wu Lianjiu, Song Huaixiang, and a woman, Lady Song Li, from Funing, on the afternoon of the day before yesterday at various locations, including Tongheli on Gordon Road, Yinghua Li on Avenue Foch, Wuchang Road, and 7 Shudeli on Hengtong Road, Zhabei. They confiscated one hundred rounds of ammunition and took them to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court. Judge Xiao Yunfen presided over the hearing. Attorney Zhang Tianyin of the police station presented the case, stating that the defendants had recently committed a kidnapping and extortion case in Zhenjiang and had hidden the hostage somewhere in Zhabei. The police are in the process of apprehending accomplices and investigating the location of the hostage. He requested that the defendants be detained. The ammunition was presented as evidence. After Judge Xiao questioned the defendants, he ordered them to be detained pending further investigation.
